Located on the Giza plateau just outside Cairo, these enormous monuments leave visitors awe-struck with their massive size and precision architecture. When visiting Egypt, a trip to the Giza pyramids is an absolute must.\n\nThe pyramids were built as elaborate tombs for the pharaohs and their queen consorts during Egypt's Old Kingdom era. The largest and oldest pyramid was constructed for Pharaoh Khufu and stands an incredible 455 feet tall! The second largest was built for Khufu's son Pharaoh Khafre. The complex also includes the smaller Pyramid of Menkaure, the Sphinx monument, temples, and worker villages.\n\nAfter arriving, tourists can behold the pyramids from a viewing area or get an even closer look by riding camels through the desert. You can literally stand right next to these immense limestone structures and gaze up at their towering height. Professional guides are on hand to provide historical context and explain the different theories of how the pyramids were constructed. Visitors can also go inside some chambers and tunnels within the pyramids to view the interior structures.\n\nIn the evening, sound and light shows are projected onto the pyramids to showcase their magnificence. This illuminates the pyramids against the night sky for a truly unforgettable sight. Make sure to take lots of pictures! The pyramid complex is an outdoor site, so plan to visit in cooler months to avoid extreme desert heat.\n\nA journey to the Great Pyramids of Giza offers the chance to reflect on the incredible achievements of ancient Egyptians while standing before their architectural grandeur. When visiting Egypt, a trip to the Giza pyramids is an absolute must.\n\nThe pyramids were built as elaborate tombs for the pharaohs and their queen consorts during Egypt's Old Kingdom era. The largest and oldest pyramid was constructed for Pharaoh Khufu and stands an incredible 455 feet tall! The second largest was built for Khufu's son Pharaoh Khafre. The complex also includes the smaller Pyramid of Menkaure, the Sphinx monument, temples, and worker villages.\n\nAfter arriving, tourists can behold the pyramids from a viewing area or get an even closer look by riding camels through the desert. You can literally stand right next to these immense limestone structures and gaze up at their towering height. Professional guides are on hand to provide historical context and explain the different theories of how the pyramids were constructed. Visitors can also go inside some chambers and tunnels within the pyramids to view the interior structures.\n\nIn the evening, sound and light shows are projected onto the pyramids to showcase their magnificence. This illuminates the pyramids against the night sky for a truly unforgettable sight. Make sure to take lots of pictures! The pyramid complex is an outdoor site, so plan to visit in cooler months to avoid extreme desert heat.\n\nA journey to the Great Pyramids of Giza offers the chance to reflect on the incredible achievements of ancient Egyptians while standing before their architectural grandeur. The old towns and tourist caf\u00e9s are also worth exploring.\n\nIn summary, with incredible natural wonders and famous tourist cities, Switzerland will surely give you an unforgettable trip. Located on the Giza plateau just outside Cairo, these enormous monuments leave visitors awe-struck with their massive size and precision architecture. When visiting Egypt, a trip to the Giza pyramids is an absolute must.\n\nThe pyramids were built as elaborate tombs for the pharaohs and their queen consorts during Egypt's Old Kingdom era. The largest and oldest pyramid was constructed for Pharaoh Khufu and stands an incredible 455 feet tall! The second largest was built for Khufu's son Pharaoh Khafre. The complex also includes the smaller Pyramid of Menkaure, the Sphinx monument, temples, and worker villages.\n\nAfter arriving, tourists can behold the pyramids from a viewing area or get an even closer look by riding camels through the desert. You can literally stand right next to these immense limestone structures and gaze up at their towering height. Professional guides are on hand to provide historical context and explain the different theories of how the pyramids were constructed. Visitors can also go inside some chambers and tunnels within the pyramids to view the interior structures.\n\nIn the evening, sound and light shows are projected onto the pyramids to showcase their magnificence. This illuminates the pyramids against the night sky for a truly unforgettable sight. Make sure to take lots of pictures! The pyramid complex is an outdoor site, so plan to visit in cooler months to avoid extreme desert heat.\n\nA journey to the Great Pyramids of Giza offers the chance to reflect on the incredible achievements of ancient Egyptians while standing before their architectural grandeur.
